04/11/22, 15:42 - +91 78006 96377: Are you wondering about ways to sharpen your mind?

 Techversity is here to assist you in oiling your skills by organising a course of "Introduction to problem solving and programming - using Python " at a very affordable cost of just ₹29(per course). 

Spending ₹1/day can provide you with an abundance of knowledge and help you take another major step to your success. 

This is time you can kick start with your code. Here we will teach you the basics . You can say with A,B,C of coding.

So, keep your worries aside and start your coding journey with Team Techversity.

Course : Introduction to problem solving and programming using python

Syllabus 

1 Introduction to Computer Problem Solving: Introduction – Problem Solving Aspect – Top-Down Design – Implementation of Algorithms (flowcharts, pseudo code, programming language) – Program Verification – Efficiency of Algorithms – Analysis of Algorithms. 

 2 Python Data, Expressions and Statements: Python interpreter and interactive mode – values and types – variables, expressions, statements, tuple assignment, precedence of operators, comments – modules and functions, function definition and use, flow of execution, parameters and arguments. 

 3 Fundamental Algorithms: Introduction – Exchange the values – Counting – Summation – Factorial Computation – Fibonacci Sequence – Reverse – Base Conversion – Character to Number Conversion Python Control Flow, Functions : Conditionals: Boolean values and operators, conditional (if, if- else, if-elif-else) – Iteration statements (state, while, for break, continue, pass); 

4 Factoring Methods: Finding square root – Smallest Divisor – GCD – Generate Prime Numbers – Computing Prime Factors – Generating Pseudo-random numbers – Raising a Number to Large Power – Computing nth 
Fibonacci Numbers 

 5 Array Techniques: Introduction – Array Order Reversal – Array Counting – Finding the Maximum number in a set – Removal of Duplicates from an ordered array – Partitioning an array – Finding the Kth smallest element Python Lists: list operations – Tuples – Sets Operations – Dictionaries – Time Tradeoff.


Classes timings will be made compatable with the students. Classes will be taken during weekend and one class during week days.
If the student ask to take more classes during week days, we will also go with it.

NOTE-TechVersity never charges for the Course manual but we are arranging for online live classes so minimal charges has been charged.
